PART III - LANDS 
 
FINAL ORDERS 
 
LAND SETTLEMENT ORDINANCE 
 
Settlement Orders No. 448 (Badulla) 
 
Whereas a settlement notice under Section 4 of the Land Settlement Ordinance was duly published in the  Gazette No. 417 of 29th Au-
gust, 1986, and as otherwise required by the said Section, in respect of the lands situated in the village of Pradhana Pradeshaya Presently 
in  Mahiyanganaya and Rideemaliyadda Divisional Sec retary‚Äôs Divisions of  Mahiyangana and Rideemaliyad da Assisstant Government 
Agent‚Äôs Divisions  of the Badulla District on the U va Province and described as Lot no. 1148 in  Block  Survey topographical Plan No. 
58 (Uva) (Vide Settlement Notice No. 5389 (Badulla)).  
 
And whereas all claims received  in pursuance of the said notice have been duly dealt with in  accordance with the provisions of the said 
Ordinance: 
 
I, the undersigned, in pursuance of the powers conf erred on me by Section 5(5) of the said Ordinance d o hereby make order that the 
lands or portions thereof be settled as specified in the Schedule to this order.  
 
 
  P.M.H.P
RIYADHARSHANI, 
  Assistant Settlement Officer 
   Commissioner of - 
  Land Title Settlement  
Given at the 
Land Title Settlement Department, 
Battaramulla This 
27th March, 2014.
